Good Girl was created by Louise Turner and Quentin Bisch. Top notes are Almond, Coffee, Bergamot and Lemon; middle notes are Tuberose, Jasmine Sambac, Orange Blossom, Bulgarian Rose and Orris; base notes are Tonka Bean, Cacao, Vanilla, Praline, Sandalwood, Musk, Amber, Cashmere Wood, Cinnamon, Patchouli and Cedar. </p><div v-pre class='fragrantica-blockquote'><p>Carolina Herrera announces the release of a new women's fragrance in September 2016. The new, sexy oriental fragrance is ironically named Good Girl with the message "It's so good to be bad!" (#goodtobebad).</p>

<p>Good Girl promises an innovative and addictive combination of tuberose and roasted tonka bean, which represents the duality of a woman’s character. A floral wave of white Sambac jasmine and tuberose is placed in contrast with the mysterious and deep notes of tonka bean and cocoa.</p>

<p>The face of the perfume is model Karlie Kloss. The fragrance comes in an elegant black stiletto shaped bottle as a 50 and 80 ml Eau de Parfum.</p>

<p>Good Girl is created by perfumers Louise Turner and Quentin Bisch.</p></div><p class="reviewstrigger" style="font-size: smaller; color: #83a6c4">Read about this perfume in other languages: <a     <div class="strike-title"><span>All Reviews By Date</span></div>
    <div class="grid-x grid-padding-x grid-margin-y" style="position: relative; padding: 0 0.25rem 0 0.25rem;">
        <div class="cell destinationreview"></div>                    <div id="parent2336695" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2336695" class="cell small-2" ><div ><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="sabinelison11"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2117446"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="sabinelison11" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2336695ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2336695" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"><div class="flex-child-shrink" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.71); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2117446">sabinelison11</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-11-03"></span><fromunixtime unixtime="1730652722" class="vote-button-legend"></fromunixtime></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I really like it. It starts off more fruity, but about 15 minutes in, it becomes warm and vanilla. It is very sweet without being too syrupy and heavy. It's a good gourmand for those just getting into gourmands. My husband doesn't like it though. He says it smells like robutussin. 😅</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39681"comment_id="2336695"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Carolina-Herrera/Good-Girl-39681.html?ccid=2336695#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2336601" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2300902" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="JolieSucre"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1233265"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1233265.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="JolieSucre" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Carolina-Herrera/Good-Girl-39681.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.39681.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Good Girl"title="Good Girl"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2300902ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2300902" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.7); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1233265">JolieSucre</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-01">10/01/24 01:40</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Not sure if I haven't already written 56 reviews of this perfume, but here it goes.<br />
<br />
It's stunning. Beautiful, creamy, sexy, feminine, rich, opulent, satiny, SWEET, sexy, even sexier, cocoa-y, creamy, SWEET, spicy, powdery, wintery, summery.... it's just absolutely stunning. Intoxicating, rich and thick, and just beautiful. A head-turner, fits every season in my view but develops best in cold weather. <br />
<br />
It's a mix of cocoa with a bit of sweet booziness from some rhum-like tang (not listed in the notes, but I definitely feel it), and some really thick and sweet musk, that really good one similar to Francis Kurkdijan's. It blends so beautifully with the tonka and the cocoa, I am so impressed particularly as other perfumes with similar notes are nothing special and not really done. <br />
<br />
Looking at Hugo Boss the brown-ish glass bottle that smells like orange chocolate, I mean that one is nothing compared to this. Unfortunately that one smells exactly like a box of orange chocolates, if you'd simply sniff the candy. Nothing special, warm, it's a badly done gourmand in my view because it smells like food and not like a perfume. <br />
<br />
Oh but this one is really special. It's one of those perfumes that mark a decade, you know, like Baccarat Rouge, or La Vie Est Belle, or Opium or Mademoiselle Coco /Dior (same thing, I promise you). It's THAT kind of scent, with such a strong personality that it is intoxicating.<br />
<br />
I've been stocking up on this + dupes as I'm afraid I'll run out :D that's how much I love it. It's just stunning and impossibly beautiful. Will wear this, Fancy by Jessica Simpson and a few of my trusted orange blossom faithfuls (5th Avenue, Eternity Moment) forever and ever.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; The scent is perfumey and nondescript.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39681"comment_id="2290236"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Carolina-Herrera/Good-Girl-39681.html?ccid=2290236#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2289502" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Not bad but I would not hunt a full bottle.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39681"comment_id="2289502"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Carolina-Herrera/Good-Girl-39681.html?ccid=2289502#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2286148" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2248073">Cymbra</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-17">09/17/24 14:03</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Decadent and a little sophisticated. It makes a statement but isn't too polarizing. I really expected to dislike this, but my nose kept coming back to my sleeve because of the rich, powdery notes. The dry down is where it really shines and mellows out perfectly. If you're just getting into gourmands, then this is a great introduction.<br />
<br />
By no means is this suitable for daytime wear, it's better for evenings during fall and winter. The lasting power is pretty decent. I sprayed this on myself in my hallway and it was lingering there hours later when I got back home. Perhaps because this also has so many components, it may not agree with everyone's skin. Definitely do a sample or try in-store before blind-buying. <br />
<br />
I also tested most of the flankers in-store, and the only other one I would consider buying is Very Good Girl. The rest smell nearly identical but not as good as the OG.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39681"comment_id="2286148"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Carolina-Herrera/Good-Girl-39681.html?ccid=2286148#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2284105" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2232554">AubreyNoel</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-15">09/15/24 18:59</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I wanted to purchase this as soon as I put it on my skin, but had I gone through with that decision it would have been a huge mistake. If there was ever a fragrance you needed to test throughout a whole day prior to purchasing, it is Good Girl.<br />
<br />
When I first put it on my skin it was EXACTLY what I was looking for, so much that I actually ran to Sephora's website to put the largest size into my cart. Something told me to hold off a little bit before placing the order, and thankfully I did, because once the scent started to turn it evolved from something beautiful to a scent that was nearly unbearable. I saw another reviewer equate the dry down to that of unwashed armpits, and I can't say that I disagree. Personally, it smells as if I rolled around on the floor of a dirty cafe then didn't shower for a few days. Needless to say it is quite awful on me. That being said, I have since smelled this on others and it smells absolutely divine on them, but unfortunately I was not blessed with the body chemistry with which this fragrance works best.<br />
<br />
In my near-constant fragrance testing these past few weeks I have been trying to figure out what note(s) in the fragrance react so poorly on me, and it seems as if it is simply a bad combination of base notes on my skin, because there really is no other explanation for why Good Girl smells so terrible on me.<br />
<br />
Lesson learned - thoroughly test a fragrance throughout an entire day before choosing to purchase.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39681"comment_id="2284105"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Carolina-Herrera/Good-Girl-39681.html?ccid=2284105#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2282519" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I feel like Good Girl smells like what we all wished Forever Krystle smelled like back in the day. My mother had a bottle of Forever Krystle and I was morbidly fascinated by it. I think my dad must have given it to her because she always displayed it on her dresser but almost never wore it. It was named after a soap opera character who was the quintessential good girl, but it smelled like Alexis must have dragged Krystle through a bordello on the way to church, it was so loud. Anyway, the scents have a lot of the same notes and seem to be meant to evoke a similar vibe, but Good Girl is more of a sweetly comforting scent than Forever Krystle ever was. I could easily imagine a real good girl wearing Good Girl. This Carolina Herrera fragrance would be a good gift for a young teen looking to try on designer scents.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39681"comment_id="2264357"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Carolina-Herrera/Good-Girl-39681.html?ccid=2264357#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2262784" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2258876" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="CandyRemi"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2203504"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2203504.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="CandyRemi" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2258876ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2258876" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.89); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2203504">CandyRemi</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-23">08/23/24 17:41</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Not necessarily what I expected but I'm glad I got this one.<br />
<br />
If i could choose one word to describe this one, "Mysterious". This is also one that I think smells like the bottle looks.<br />
<br />
On the first spray I definitely get citrus, almond and floral. It smells like a mirage of a very bright cheerful perfume but very quickly that dies down into something else.<br />
<br />
I can't pick out specific notes while I wear this one, but it is powdery and sweet once the top notes are gone. Faintly smells like fruit loops which I like.<br />
<br />
To me this is sexy, but not overtly sexy. I kind of imagine a mysterious girl in a black dress giving you looks from across the room. You can't really tell what she's thinking. If you are lucky enough to spend the night with her, no words are exchanged, everything becomes a blur, like you are under some sort of spell. padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2240230" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="StrangeTrails"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2138040"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2138040.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="StrangeTrails" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Atelier-Cologne/Santal-Carmin-25292.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.25292.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Santal Carmin"title="Santal Carmin"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2240230ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2240230" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.73); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2138040">StrangeTrails</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-05">08/05/24 22:41</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Goodness this perfume has a lot going on in it. <br />
<br />
On initial open, it smells almost aquatic to me - it kind of has a "fresh" male cologne vibe that doesn't read feminine at all to me, I think it's coming from the bergamot and the jasmine/orange blossom. I do not get coffee or almond at all in the open - maybe a hint of almond in the form of an almond milk vibe, but only faintly. This lasts for maybe 30 minutes on me.<br />
<br />
Then the patchouli hits, and it hits like a TRAIN. There's vanilla too - maybe some musk, a bit of amber, and oh yeah. Orris. Here comes the powder explosion at the end of the eye-watering, maybe even slightly nauseating mid tones. I think the Tuberose is backing that Orris baby powder bomb as well, so you get an almost grandmotherly boudoir white floral sneezefest for a bit. <br />
<br />
If you survived all that, maybe an hour into the drydown, the suddenly the heavens open up. The sneezefest baby powder takes a back seat. The patchouli smooths out to a velvety whisper in the background. The vanilla opens up, along with a sexy jasmine, and then a backbone of warm cacao. The almond and coffee I never got in the opening suddenly pull through, in supporting roles for the vanilla and cacao. I can't distinguish much between the Tonka and Vanilla, I think they kind of blend into one another when used together, but it's soft and feminine. You have whiplash from the sudden departure of those salty aquatic citrus notes that screeched at you through the whole opening. <br />
<br />
All in all I think it's super weird. You can kinda see a comparison between this and the Roberto Cavalli Signature line Louise Turner did in the DNA. I get the people saying this is too much going on - it has a kind of neurotic frantic evolution for what is essentially a jasmine-tinged gourmand. But it's also kind of addicting! It's Good Girl if your Good Girl is a kind of stressed out overachieving horse girl with ADHD who kind of bites off more than she can chew and also has some weird leather kink she indulges in once in a blue moon.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; I found "Gold Spell Mist from Eva Skin care Egyption brand" the mentioned mist have a dupe calm scent.<br />

<br />

This is coming from someone who has a collection of sweet and girly perfumes, so this is taking me to another level and making me feel more grown.  It can be strong, and it leans masculine (another irony) to my nose.  It’s best for date nights and colder days.<br />
<br />
For a gourmand, it’s a clean smell.  Someone mentioned in their review that it reminded them of fabric softener, and I can totally smell that.  At the same time, there is something that is making this warm and cozy.  It must be the tonka bean, cacao, vanilla and almond combination, although I would have never been able to pinpoint any one, if it were not for Fragrantica’s note breakdown.<br />
<br />
As I mentioned in my Good Girl Blush review, the bottle is what’s hindering me from purchasing this fragrance.  It’s a bit…much.  Then again, I could always look for the travel size version.  But there’s also something about the stiletto that wholly encapsulates the fragrance…and I think I might be getting accustomed to it now.<br />
<br />

I've got nothing against rich compositions or bold perfumes, but this one is a nauseating mishmash, as if someone had tried to cook a dish with leftovers that don't mix well. We're a long way from a bold but thoughtful composition with notes that tone each other down : in here, there's too much of everything. Too much citrus, too much floral, too much gourmand, too much woods. This is the only perfume that reminds me of that feeling of being sick and having a fever: I feel hot but also cold at the same time, and I hate it! <br />
In addition to being all overdosed, the notes smell like cheap synthetics, leaning towards a restroom freshener... Really, I can't. A strong perfume for the sake of being strong, with no structure or identity. If vulgarity were a perfume, it would be Good Girl. And I'm not even talking about the bottle.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39681"comment_id="2211162"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Carolina-Herrera/Good-Girl-39681.html?ccid=2211162#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2208807" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; It is overwhelming! Nothing for the first few seconds - and then - wham! All the notes came thundering in at the same time. Okay, not at once. It did get stronger and stronger and stronger.... It also hung around for a very long time - long after I left the room. Not even twenty minutes of scrubbing would remove it... So, while I do not love this offering, I am bowled over by it. A fragrance for all the Good Girls in the world wherever they may be. A fragrance for dark, cold evenings . An offering for romantic evenings and most certainly for hot, sizzling dates. Good luck, Ladies</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39681"comment_id="2201151"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Carolina-Herrera/Good-Girl-39681.html?ccid=2201151#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2199878" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2176531">oliwiakuchar</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-26">06/26/24 05:48</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>When I first smelled Carolina Herrera Good Girl Perfume at a local store, I thought it was very average. Knowing that everyone seemed to wear it, I felt compelled to try it. After checking the notes on Fragrantica, I was stunned to see so many sweet notes listed, as it didn't seem sweet to me at all. So, I returned to the store, specifically searching for those sweet notes, but I still couldn't detect them. Instead, it smelled like regular soap to me—nothing interesting, just a standard soap scent. This left me quite discouraged, and I didn't think fondly of the perfume until I tried my grandma's test tube version.<br />
<br />
That was a turning point. The test tube smelled like sweet cinnamon with a hint of something spicy and some floral notes. This experience gave me a new perspective, so I went back to the store to see if the larger bottle there would smell the same. I paid attention to the volume of liquid in the bottle, hoping it had macerated for at least a month, considering it was from a less popular store. Unfortunately, the scent from the larger bottle didn't impress me. It smelled a bit similar, but still not quite right.<br />
<br />
I know my grandma got her test tube a long time ago, so perhaps the formula has changed. Despite this, I just don't get the hype surrounding this perfume. It's just average in my opinion, and if it weren't for the price, I might consider buying it. However, I'm sure you can find a similar scent for much less, around twenty dollars probably.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39681"comment_id="2199878"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Carolina-Herrera/Good-Girl-39681.html?ccid=2199878#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2197810" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2070359">jilly9</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-05-12">05/12/24 20:50</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I say this as someone who loves heady floral fragrances — this was too much for me. There’s too much going on in this fragrance, and I think it’s the combination of indolic white florals and bergamot that’s scratching my nose the wrong way. The bergamot note in this is very screechy, and it’s all I could smell on first spray — I didn’t get any almond or coffee. I could finally detect the almond and vanilla on the dry down after quite a while, but I find the creamier notes in this to be overshadowed by the really sharp bergamot and florals.<br />
<br />
I agree with the below reviewer who called this the Frankenstein of perfumes — it’s as if the perfumer just haphazardly combined all of the most popular fragrance notes. I don’t agree that this is a “boss lady” office fragrance as some have asserted. It’s definitely mature but not in an elegant or classy way. It’s giving classy and trashy at the same time, like what I would imagine a high end brothel smells like.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39681"comment_id="2154104"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Carolina-Herrera/Good-Girl-39681.html?ccid=2154104#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2152708" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/868046">emdash</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-04-29">04/29/24 10:00</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>She seems like an innocent powdery floral when you first meet her, but as the night wears on, a slightly unexpected vampy side comes out. She's the girl who takes off her birth control glasses, lets down her bun, and transforms into a bombshell.<br />
<br />
Look, I am sometimes an embarrassingly late adopter of certain designer scents. Pretty sure I sprayed this on a card when it was released, didn't like it for some reason, and have spent the last eight years wondering why it has been so popular. Until yesterday when I happened upon a sample and tried it on my actual skin. I am now intoxicated by this enigmatic scent.<br />
<br />
I was stunned to learn that the opening smells like the original Caress body wash, of which I have fond core memories. Interestingly, the only note these two apparently share is orange blossom (but who really knows what goes into a drugstore body wash). After the blast of Caress, this softens and deepens and spirals into a spicy and bittersweet gourmand. A hint of powdery floral remains, leaving me to wonder how these two fragrances, one good and one naughty, can be one and the same. I want more.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39681"comment_id="2140055"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Carolina-Herrera/Good-Girl-39681.html?ccid=2140055#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2139476" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; But I have it now, and to be honest I do like it and I have been getting several compliments but for me I feel like it doesn't last longer than an hour. I spray it on my neck, wrists, and chest but after a while I can't even smell it. Or maybe it's just my nose getting used to the smell. <br />
<br />
I usually use scents that suit my age, that are more feminine, sweet and candy like. I'd say some perfumes from Ariana Grande or Victoria's Secret body mists. But this was a bit new, even though it is feminine and a base note of vanilla. I feel it gives off more a mature woman type of feeling and vibe. <br />
<br />
When I first spray it: I get a strong sandalwood and a strong floral smell. I'd say it also has a bit of masculinity in it. But for me it's not very smooth and clean. It's more of a mature and stronger scent. So if that's what you like then you'll probably like. For instance my mothers friend who would be around 30-35 years old absolutely loved the scent, and she kept sniffing it and asked me what the name of the perfume was. I just don't understand the hype around it though. And neither do I understand why men like it so much. I'm not hating on it because it's really not that bad at all. But to be honest Iv'e smelled better. <br />
<br />
And yes, it does make you feel badass and hot. But I don't think it's a signature scent kind of perfume for me. Though it's good for gatherings, dates or parties. I just wouldn't wear this to school or shopping. I'd go for something more simple and less mature.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39681"comment_id="2130441"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Carolina-Herrera/Good-Girl-39681.html?ccid=2130441#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2127966" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I didn't know much about perfumery at the time, so if I did not like a fragrance on the first application, I would decide it's not for me and leave it at that. The coffee top note, old-fashioned white floral middle notes and tacky packaging did not help the situation...<br />
<br />
I've worn it on casual occasions since then... and it has grown on me. It's not a bad perfume at all. Someone down below said it well: this was made with mass appeal in mind. The base notes are what I personally like about GG, and it now makes sense why: it's because I loooooooooooove gourmand scents.<br />
<br />
My horrible step-grandma (?) complimented me for the first time, specifically the way I smell, when I wore this layered with a sparkly body spray (Bi Es Blossom Avenue; someone said this is extremely similar to La Nuit Tresor).<br />
<br />
I would say this makes a good gift for an average young (20-40 years old) woman. It's not amazing but not terrible either. I could see it being used effectively in any situation (casual or formal). The longevity and sillage are good, but it costs too much for what it offers, in my honest opinion.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39681"comment_id="2126601"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Carolina-Herrera/Good-Girl-39681.html?ccid=2126601#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2125330" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:1,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2111943" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Indulgence"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1197661"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1197661.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Indulgence" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Maison-Francis-Kurkdjian/Le-Beau-Parfum-34026.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.34026.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Le Beau Parfum"title="Le Beau Parfum"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2111943ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2111943" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.9); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1197661">Indulgence</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-04-02">04/02/24 10:58</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>To me this smells like a safe office scent (just don’t overspray!) and like a more mature less sweet version of Ari from Ariana Grande. It’s just okay to me, pleasant enough. I personally don’t find it sexy but totally understand those who feel that way. <br />
<br />
I can’t smell the lemon or bergamot. To me, the vanilla, almonds, Tonka beans, (very creamy) sandalwood, white florals, amber, and musk are the most prominent notes. The rest all blends together. The almond note doesn’t smell artificial, it smells like real almonds and it’s not overpowering. <br />
<br />
Upon first spraying it I can see why people see it as a generic basic perfume. I think where GG really shines is in the dry down. It makes me feel like I’m wearing a second skin and it’s very pretty, pleasant, subtly sweet, and comforting. <br />
<br />
I doubt I will ever finish the bottle since I rarely reach for it but if I do I wouldn’t bother repurchasing it. It just doesn’t wow me even though I can see the appeal.<br />
<br />
Note: It’s very powdery to me, just a warning for anyone who doesn’t love feeling like they’re burying their faces in foundation powder.<br />
<br />
Update: I tried Mod Blush by Ariana Grande and it smells very similar to that perfume as well. People are saying it’s more like Good Girl Blush. So keep that in mind if you like that one!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39681"comment_id="2111943"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Carolina-Herrera/Good-Girl-39681.html?ccid=2111943#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2111081" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2049689">isolaviola</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-04-01">04/01/24 14:54</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Sad to say I don't see the appeal. Initial spray gives nothing interesting to suck you in. I get the jasmine and the tiniest hint of the lemon and that's it. Dry down all I can smell is light musk and cashmere, and the abundance of base notes all mix together to give a homogenised smell that doesn't give anything identifiably specific. I can see why people might enjoy it - there's something of a subtle sexiness to it, but it gives more attractive hotel hostess than maneater. Probably  a good work scent which is funny considering how outlandish and tacky the bottle is. The rest of it is a generic cool artificial scent that is inoffensive and honestly smells very similar to many more affordable fragrances. Maybe I'm simply guilty of only enjoying fragrances that pack a dramatic punch in their top notes, but this one gives much to be desired. I think men enjoy this one simply because it is very reminiscent of the generic male aftershave scent, but more feminine. Something about it reminds me vaguely of Alien, but devoid of everything that makes Alien unique. To those who aren't fragrance obsessed maybe this is a hit, but when you know there's much more interesting choices on the market it falls to the wayside for me.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; I like it but it's not groundbreaking or original or anything</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39681"comment_id="2092844"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Carolina-Herrera/Good-Girl-39681.html?ccid=2092844#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2091665" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.85);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2091665" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Enrium"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/36833"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.36833.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Enrium" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Glossier/You-46885.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.46885.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="You"title="You"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2091665ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2091665" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.85); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/36833">Enrium</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-03-13">03/13/24 14:34</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Good Girl is generic, sweet feminine scent, designed with mass appeal in mind. The only thing that sets it apart is its kitsch stiletto-shaped bottle, but I find the entire experience of this scent cheap and gimmicky. Although, as a designer floral gourmand, GG needs something to make itself stand out. While it's not my thing, I've smelled worse.<br />
<br />
GG is vanilla-dominant from initial spray, with the almond note up top giving a nutty, gourmand quality. I get a sprinkle of coffee up top, adding a spiced chocolate-y edge, Black Opium-style.<br />
<br />
Sweet white florals creep in, notably jasmine, with some watery freesia following. The tuberose is uncharacteristically subtle, but the orange blossom that follows more than makes up for it, syrupy and tropical. It becomes powdery as it progresses, with a prominent cocoa note adding to the gourmand theme. I don't get rose or iris notes as such, but they perhaps add to the powdery heart. <br />
<br />
Coumarin takes over from the almond opening, adding a smooth, Play-Doh-like quality to the base. This alongside the powdery cacao and syrupy vanilla gives a praline effect. It fades to a musky vanilla skin scent. Sillage and longevity are moderate. It is a feminine autumn/winter scent.<br />
<br />
GG becomes thin fairly quickly, despite its bold vanilla-floral profile and plethora of gourmand notes. Unsurprisingly, it smells quite cheap - synthetic and syrupy, but not nasty. It reminds me in parts of many other designer offerings. Buy Hypnotic Poison instead. 2/5.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39681"comment_id="2091665"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Carolina-Herrera/Good-Girl-39681.html?ccid=2091665#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2087821" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.87);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; With some gleeful help from the patchouli.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39681"comment_id="2064884"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Carolina-Herrera/Good-Girl-39681.html?ccid=2064884#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2057542" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; To me, this is THE best female perfume I've put my nose to yet. <br />
<br />
Girlfriend came home with a sample one day, and as I was sniffing it, I instantly knew; this is the #1 female frag. Didn't have to re-evaluate, didn't have to double take, didn't have to go all snobby and search for this and that note/accord - it was just instinctively glorious. I've been smelling that sample each and every single day until she bought a full bottle.<br />
<br />
Super well composed, addicting, balanced to perfection. Really high quality dna. <br />
<br />
I don't get why CH had to make such a kickass bottle, seems overkill - I mean, this could come in a Heinz baked beans can and I'd be equally impressed.<br />
<br />
* Signature worthy: yes.<br />
* All occasions: yes.<br />
* Age: won't matter.<br />
* Blind buy worthy: yes.<br />
<br />
Louise Turner, you are a flippin' genious. Please make a "Good Guy". Please. I'll help you kickstart it or whatever.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39681"comment_id="913527"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Carolina-Herrera/Good-Girl-39681.html?ccid=913527#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1072851" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/267115">Safira</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2019-06-24">06/24/19 12:15</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>It's like it's slightly trendy to belittle this perfume. "The bottle is too tacky", "the notes are generic" and so on. Well, I went in with an open mind and with a couple of hundred perfumes 'under my belt', I have to say, this is pretty unique. <br />
<br />
When I first tried it on, I felt like it was all over the place. This perfume packs a lot of notes, and I get why people can feel overwhelmed. I do, however, feel like the notes combine beautifully, and this is a very comforting scent. It's perfect for autumn and winter, but although today is a hot summer evening, it's still gorgeous. I get mostly tonka, almond and white florals (no cacao really) and I love that it's got great longevity.<br />
<br />
Also, I'll confess... I love the bottle. It's kitschy and just right. :)</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39681"comment_id="1072851"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Carolina-Herrera/Good-Girl-39681.html?ccid=1072851#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent759267" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/57880">Whit</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2016-11-07">11/07/16 22:49</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I'm really amazed at all the negative reviews concerning this perfume. I think it's lovely! I mean, sure, it's not groundbreaking, but it's not that bad either. I get mostly the tonka and cacao on me, with nuances of the white florals. I can't believe there's no vanilla in this; it has to be the way the notes are mixing on my skin because I get vanilla as well. I think the bottle is cool too; it's different. I will say that the name "Good Girl" fits it, because she's not a bad bitch at all. She's quite nice, friendly, sweet and pink is her favorite color. I actually love this scent so much that I bought a backup of it already. I find it cozy, sweet and warm. Longevity on me is awesome, lasting into the next day. Sillage is somewhat big at first, but settles to a more moderate aroma. Based on my skin, I would classify it as a floral-oriental with a gourmand twist. CH's perfumes usually work well on my skin and this was another winner for me. Thanks CH for another lovely perfume!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39681"comment_id="759267"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Carolina-Herrera/Good-Girl-39681.html?ccid=759267#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent824125" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1058723">timventura</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2017-05-19">05/19/17 10:38</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This is destined to be THE women's fragrance of 2017. My wife has samples of like 30 designer &amp; niche perfumes, and this is my absolute favorite. Totally dead sexy fragrance.<br />
<br />
I dropped by Macy's to buy her a full bottle for her birthday yesterday, and the counter-girl said they're selling it so fast they can't keep it on the shelves - and I believe it.<br />
<br />
It's a sleek, modern fragrance with a powdery, clean scent - but underneath that there's that sexy tuberose just waiting to tantalize the nose &amp; draw you in. That's my "sales pitch" for it  :o)<br />
<br />
I actually bought this sample for my wife a few weeks back. I've been reading how incredibly sexy Tuberose is, so I got her a sample of Fracas - and was literally taken aback by how incredibly strong &amp; cloying Fracas is. It smells VERY dated, not surprising for a 70-year-old formula.<br />
<br />
So I blind-bought a sample of "Good Girl", was a little scared by some of the "so so" reviews online, then forgot about it until she put it on. Absolutely amazing! It integrates tuberose - isn't overwhelmed by it. That's exactly what I wanted.<br />
<br />
So "Good Girl" is a great description for this, because on top is IS a "Good Girl" fragrance - but underneath it's just a little bit Bad Girl, which is basically what CH marketing said.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; The tonka, combined with flowers, creates a nauseating effect for me. It's not too floral, it's not too creamy, it's not too gourmand, it's like a really long lasting, generic, all over the place mess.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1060084">fancyvivid</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2021-10-24">10/24/21 09:05</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I got a tester of this and tried it as an evening perfume. If I were to place this on the alignment chart it would be chaotic evil. There is far too much going on and none of it is good. It is bitingly strong, cluttered, headache-inducing, and absolutely disharmonious. In fact, it gave me a headache that lasted almost as long as this perfume. I would describe this scent as an evil, sadistic dominatrix, who has absolutely no clue what she's doing and therefore currently has several people locked up in her basement, who may or may not be dying. I can recommend this scent to anyone who has lost their sense of smell due to covid, as I think you might be able to revive it with this perfume.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="39681"comment_id="1433762"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Carolina-Herrera/Good-Girl-39681.html?ccid=1433762#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div>                            <reviews-infinity :random-colors="[&quot;#fefcee&quot;,&quot;#faf7ec&quot;,&quot;#f9f9f3&quot;,&quot;#f8f9ec&quot;,&quot;#fffdea&quot;,&quot;#faf9fb&quot;,&quot;#faf5f2&quot;,&quot;#f7f4f2&quot;]" :perfume-id="39681" sentiment="negative"></reviews-infinity>
